<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напряженный.html>напряжённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naprjažónnyj</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напрячь.html>напря́чь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naprjáčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>intense, intensive</li>
<li>strained</li>
<li>arduous <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">needing or using up much energy</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напрячь.html>напря́чь</a> (12827)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-прячь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-prjačʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напрячь.html>напря́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naprjáčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напрягать.html>напряга́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flex (a muscle)</li>
<li>to strain (the back, the ears)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stress out</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напускать.html>напуска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napuskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напустить.html>напусти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let in, to allow to enter (a large amount of liquid, gas or small items)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to let in (someone)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:напускать.html>напуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>napuskátʹ</b> na sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to feign, to affect (a trait)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:напускать.html>напуска́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>napuskátʹ</b> tumánu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to confuse the issue</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to unleash, to sic (an animal) on; to incite (someone) onto <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike, to incite (fear, etc.) in <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***напустить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напустить.html>напусти́ть</a> (19656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напустить.html>напусти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napustítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напускать.html>напуска́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let in, to allow to enter (a large amount of liquid, gas or small items)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to let in (someone)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:напустить.html>напусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>napustítʹ</b> na sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to feign, to affect (a trait)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:напустить.html>напусти́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туман.html>тума́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>napustítʹ</b> tumánu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to confuse the issue</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to unleash, to sic (an animal) on; to incite (someone) onto <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike, to incite (fear, etc.) in <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***напутавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напутавший.html>напу́тавший</a> (15982)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напутавший.html>напу́тавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napútavšij</span>)
</p>

***напутствие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напутствие.html>напу́тствие</a> (23224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напутствие.html>напу́тствие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napútstvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напутствие.html>напу́тствия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напутствие.html>напу́тствия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напутствие.html>напу́тствий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>parting words, parting wishes</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напутствие.html>напу́тствие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">napútstvije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***напяливать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напяливать.html>напя́ливать</a> (22280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напялить.html>напя́лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">napjálitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напяливать.html>напя́ливать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napjálivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напялить.html>напя́лить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch <i>(on)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull <i>(on)</i>, to get on</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular<span class="ib-comma">,</span> deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trick out <i>(in)</i>, to dude up <i>(in)</i>, to fig up, to fig out <i>(in)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напялить.html>напя́лить</a> (14101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пялить.html>пя́лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjálitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напялить.html>напя́лить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napjálitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напяливать.html>напя́ливать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch <i>(on)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull <i>(on)</i>, to get on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>стара́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:напялить.html>напя́лить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:слишком.html>сли́шком</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тесный.html>те́сное</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">starátʹsja <b>napjálitʹ</b> na sebjá štó-libo slíškom tésnoje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to squeeze/struggle into smth that is too small for one</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular<span class="ib-comma">,</span> deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to trick out <i>(in)</i>, to dude up <i>(in)</i>, to fig up, to fig out <i>(in)</i></li></ol>

***наработать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наработать.html>нарабо́тать</a> (25340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наработать.html>нарабо́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">narabótatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нараба́тывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to work <i>(a period of time)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to acquire
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наработать.html>нарабо́тать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:опыт.html>о́пыт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narabótatʹ</b> ópyt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to gain experience</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наравне.html>наравне́</a> (14903)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:равно.html>равно́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ravnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наравне.html>наравне́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naravné</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>on a level <i>(with)</i></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нараспев.html>нараспе́в</a> (19135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">распе́в</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raspév</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нараспев.html>нараспе́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naraspév</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>in a singsong manner, liltingly, melodically <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of speech</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
